| 230| `SelectiveRestoreCoordinatorTests.progress_movesMonotonically_through3Phases` is a flaky test — `#expect(values.last == 1.0)` intermittently fails with `values.last → 0.85` under CPU load | Tests/Backup | Low | FIXED | **FIXED 2026-05-21 in v3.38.40** — replaced the detached-`Task`-per-callback recorder + `Task.yield()` drain with a synchronous lock-guarded `final class Collector: @unchecked Sendable`. The `progress` param is `@Sendable (Double) -> Void` called synchronously by the coordinator, so recording inline (`progress: { v in collector.record(v) }`) guarantees every value is captured in call order by the time `restoreSelectively` returns — no detached Task, no `Task.yield()` race. Verified deterministic: 5/5 consecutive isolated runs green. Test-only change; production progress reporting untouched. **Filed 2026-05-19 by the Bug #225 / GH #911 `/fix-issue` run** during post-merge close-gate verification (observed once on merged `origin/main` commit `ad66db1`, in a combined 2-suite run; passes 3/3 in isolation-suite runs). **Separate defect from Bug #225** — does NOT involve `NotificationCenter` cross-test pollution at all, so it was out of #225's scope and is filed separately per the working agreement (discover-a-bug → file, don't fix in an unrelated PR). Bug #225's row mentioned this test as "intermittently affected" but mis-attributed it to the global-`NotificationCenter` race; the actual mechanism is internal to this test. **Root cause**: the test feeds `restoreSelectively`'s `progress:` closure with `{ v in Task { await collector.record(v) } }` — each progress callback spawns a **detached unstructured `Task`** that records into a `Collector` actor. The test then does `await Task.yield()` twice and reads `await collector.values`. `Task.yield()` is not a synchronization primitive — it does not guarantee previously-spawned detached `Task`s have run; under load the final callback's `Task` (recording `1.0`) has not executed when the test reads `values`, so `values.last` is the penultimate value `0.85`. **Fix direction**: make the test deterministically await all progress callbacks before asserting — collect progress values synchronously in the closure (no detached `Task`), OR make `restoreSelectively`'s `progress` closure `async` and `await`-ed so the final callback completes before the call returns. Bare `Task.yield()` must be replaced. **Severity Low** — test-only flake; production progress reporting is unaffected; the test passes in isolation. GH: #954 |

The non-timer chunked clear paths simply do not exist — different trigger, pre-existing, out of #154's scope (discover-a-bug → file, don't fix in an unrelated PR). **Fix direction**: give the chunked path parity with `TXTTextViewBridgeCoordinator` — register a `.searchHighlightClear` observer in `Coordinator.init`, add a user-driven scroll-clear gated on `isTracking || isDragging || isDecelerating` (the canonical signal from bug #99), route both through a shared clear helper that calls `clearHighlight(in:)`, resets `lastHighlightRange`, and fires `onTemporaryHighlightCleared?()` once. | 236| `XCUITestMockSpeechSynthesizerTests.speakCompletesWithDidFinish` is a flaky test — asserts the mock's synthetic timeline finished after a bare `Task.sleep(3.5s)`; intermittently fails (`delegate.didFinishCount → 0`, `mock.isSpeaking → true`) when the shared simulator is under CPU contention | Tests/TTS | Low | FIXED | **Renumbered #234 → #235 → #236 — successive ID collisions: #234 taken by PR #981's TXT-TOC bug, then #235 taken by a concurrently-triaged AZW3 cross-chapter-scroll bug; both merged before this row landed. Filed 2026-05-19 by the feature #58 WI-1 Gate-3 full-suite test gate** (`feat/feature-58-wi-1-stats-models`, observed against a clean WI-1 build whose only changes are three new pure-value-type files). Same flaky-test defect class as Bug #230 — a test-only timing flake, NOT a regression and NOT a product defect. **Symptom**: in a full `xcodebuild test -only-testing:vreaderTests` run the suite intermittently reports 2–12 failures concentrated in `XCUITestMockSpeechSynthesizerTests` (always) and `BackgroundIndexingCoordinatorTests` (sometimes). `speakCompletesWithDidFinish` fails `#expect(delegate.didFinishCount == 1)` (got 0) and `#expect(mock.isSpeaking == false)` (got true). **Non-deterministic**: two back-to-back full-suite runs produced 12 then 2 failures; both suites pass 3/3 in isolation (`-only-testing:vreaderTests/XCUITestMockSpeechSynthesizerTests` → 19 tests, 0 failures). **Root cause**: `speakCompletesWithDidFinish` does `mock.speak(utterance)` then `try await Task.sleep(nanoseconds: 3_500_000_000)` and immediately asserts the mock's internal synthetic-timeline callbacks (`didFinish`) have fired. `Task.sleep` is wall-clock, not a synchronization primitive — when the simulator is starved (vreader runs 4 booted sims; sibling Gate-3 agents build in parallel), the mock's internal timer driving the synthetic timeline does not advance far enough in 3.5 s wall-clock, so `didFinish` has not been delivered when the assertion runs. This is exactly `.claude/rules/10-tdd.md`'s documented anti-pattern ("Bare `Task.sleep(...)` for sync → flaky in CI → use `XCTestExpectation` with timeout"). `BackgroundIndexingCoordinatorTests`' 10 intermittent failures (`status → .indexing` instead of `.indexed`, `count → 0`) are the same class — async work unfinished at assert time under load. **Repro**: run the full `vreaderTests` suite while other simulator-bound work runs concurrently; `speakCompletesWithDidFinish` fails ~50–100% of the time; in isolation it passes. **Fix direction**: replace the bare `Task.sleep`-then-assert with a deterministic wait on the actual completion signal — an `XCTestExpectation` fulfilled by the `RecordingDelegate`'s `didFinish` callback with a generous `fulfillment(of:timeout:)`, OR have the mock expose an `async` "timeline finished" awaitable the test can `await` directly. Apply the same fix shape to `BackgroundIndexingCoordinatorTests`' load-sensitive cases. **Severity Low** — test-only flake; `XCUITestMockSpeechSynthesizer` is a DEBUG/UITest helper (never in Release), production TTS is unaffected, and both suites pass in isolation. | 238| No DebugBridge search-driver — `DebugCommand` has no `search` case, the harness cannot drive a search query + result tap CU-free | DevTools/Verification | Medium | FIXED | **FIXED 2026-05-20** (branch `fix/issue-976-debugbridge-search-driver`). Robustness: `@State debugBridgeSearchTask` serializes commands (a second URL cancels the first; `.onDisappear` also cancels — late completion can never fire after the reader closes); `expectedQuery` guard on the result-poll bails when a later URL overwrote the shared `query`; iterative pagination via `loadMore()` until `results.count > index` or `hasMore == false` (Medium #3 audit fix); 30s index-wait + 15s result-wait budgets.
